        function logAssetError(e) {

                location = '',

                url = 'unknown',
                data = '',
                message = 'Asset loading error';
            try {
                referer = document.referer;

            try {
                location = document.location.href;

                app: 'www',
                language: 'en_US'

                    xhr.open("POST", "/report/message", true);

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(window).load(function() {
    // adjust install links
    var usePaidLink = window.location.search.indexOf('pre=paid') !== -1;
    var useTradeLink = window.location.search.indexOf('pre=trade') !== -1;
    var partnerType = usePaidLink ? 'paid' : useTradeLink ? 'trade' : 'default';
    var entryPoint = 'splash';

    var getRequestingDevice = function() {
      if (isAndroid() || isIos()) {
        return 'mobile';
      } else {
        return 'desktop';
      }
    }

    var getMobileDownloadLink = function(partnerType, requestingDevice, targetPlatfom, entryPoint) {
      // pasting this from SPA because, frankly, who can figure out how to reuse a piece of javascript in this framework?
      //var pre, requestingDevice;
      //requestingDevice = this.isMobile() ? 'mobile' : 'desktop';
      pre = partnerType + '.' + requestingDevice + '.' + targetPlatfom + '.' + entryPoint;
      switch (pre) {
        case 'default.mobile.ios.vtb':
          return "https://app.adjust.com/tj6ui0?campaign=organic_banner";
        case 'default.mobile.ios.splash':
          return "https://app.adjust.com/tj6ui0?campaign=organic_splash";
        case 'default.mobile.android.vtb':
          return "https://app.adjust.com/bdwiqo?campaign=organic_banner";
        case 'default.mobile.android.splash':
          return "https://app.adjust.com/bdwiqo?campaign=organic_splash";
        case 'default.desktop.ios.vtb':
          return "https://app.adjust.com/knizob?campaign=organic";
        case 'default.desktop.ios.splash':
          throw new Error("mobile splash not supported on desktop");
          break;
        case 'default.desktop.android.vtb':
          return "https://app.adjust.com/33ldak?campaign=organic";
        case 'default.desktop.android.splash':
          throw new Error("mobile splash not supported on desktop");
          break;
        case 'paid.mobile.ios.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/tj6ui0?campaign=paid_banner';
        case 'paid.mobile.ios.splash':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/tj6ui0?campaign=paid_splash';
        case 'paid.mobile.android.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/bdwiqo?campaign=paid_banner';
        case 'paid.mobile.android.splash':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/bdwiqo?campaign=paid_splash';
        case 'paid.desktop.ios.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/knizob?campaign=paid';
        case 'paid.desktop.ios.splash':
          throw new Error("mobile splash not supported on desktop");
          break;
        case 'paid.desktop.android.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/33ldak?campaign=paid';
        case 'paid.desktop.android.splash':
          throw new Error("mobile splash not supported on desktop");
          break;
        case 'trade.mobile.ios.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/tj6ui0?campaign=partner_trade';
        case 'trade.mobile.ios.splash':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/tj6ui0?campaign=partner_trade';
        case 'trade.mobile.android.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/bdwiqo?campaign=partner_trade';
        case 'trade.mobile.android.splash':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/bdwiqo?campaign=partner_trade';
        case 'trade.desktop.ios.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/knizob?campaign=partner_trade';
        case 'trade.desktop.ios.splash':
          throw new Error("mobile splash not supported on desktop");
          break;
        case 'trade.desktop.android.vtb':
          return 'https://app.adjust.com/33ldak?campaign=partner_trade';
        case 'trade.desktop.android.splash':
          throw new Error("mobile splash not supported on desktop");
          break;
        default:
          throw new Error("link not found for " + pre);
      };
    };

    var getAndroidLink = function() {
      var requestingDevice = getRequestingDevice();
      return getMobileDownloadLink(partnerType, requestingDevice, 'android', entryPoint);
    }

    var getIOSLink = function() {
      var requestingDevice = getRequestingDevice();
      return getMobileDownloadLink(partnerType, requestingDevice, 'ios', entryPoint);
    }

    // Display IOS download popup to IOS users.  Bassed on presence on cookie and device type.
    var isIos = function() {
      return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i)
              || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i)
              || navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i);
    }

    // Display Android download popup to Android users.  Bassed on presence on cookie and device type.
    var isAndroid = function() {
      return navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i);
    }

    var hidePinnedFooter = function() {
      cookie.set("mobile-footer", true, {expires: 1}); // 1 day until it can be shown again
      jQuery('.splash-footer:first').removeClass('footer-visible');
    };

    var showPinnedFooter = function() {
      var downloadUrl;
      if (isIos()) {
        downloadUrl = getIOSLink();
      }
      if (isAndroid()) {
        downloadUrl = getAndroidLink();
      }
      if (!cookie.get("mobile-footer")) {
        jQuery('.splash-footer').find('.download-link:first').attr('href', downloadUrl);
        jQuery('.splash-footer').addClass('footer-visible');

        jQuery('.close-footer-container').on('touchstart', function() {
          hidePinnedFooter();
        });
      }
    };

    var showingModal = false;
    if (!cookie.get("mobile-popup") &amp;&amp; isIos()) {
      showingModal = true;

      jQuery('body').addClass('height-auto');
      jQuery('#tb-stumble-frame').hide();

      cookie.set("mobile-popup", true, {expires: 1}); // 1 day until it can be shown again
      $("body").append(jQuery("#ios-template").html());
      $('.ios-link').attr('href', getIOSLink());

    } else if (!cookie.get("mobile-popup") &amp;&amp; isAndroid()) {
      showingModal = true;

      jQuery('body').addClass('height-auto');
      jQuery('#tb-stumble-frame').hide();

      cookie.set("mobile-popup", true, {expires: 1}); // 1 day until it can be shown again
      $("body").append(jQuery("#android-template").html());
      $('.android-link').attr('href', getAndroidLink());
    }

    // Show pinned footer after close the popup to iOS / Android users
    jQuery('.splash .close-btn').on('click', function() {
      jQuery('#tb-stumble-frame').show();
      jQuery('body').removeClass('height-auto');
      jQuery('.splash').css('display', 'none');

      cookie.remove("mobile-footer")
      $("body").append(jQuery('#fixed-footer').html());
      setTimeout(function() {
        showPinnedFooter();
      }, 3000);
    });

    // Show pinned footer always only for iOS / Android users
    if (!showingModal &amp;&amp; (isIos() || isAndroid())) {
      $("body").append(jQuery('#fixed-footer').html());
      showPinnedFooter();
    }
  });
  </script>
